## SHLVL

–ú–æ–¥—É–ª—å `shlvl` –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É—î –ø–æ—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–π [`SHLVL`](https://tldp.org/LDP/abs/html/internalvariables.html#SHLVLREF) ('shell level') –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—É –æ—Ç–æ—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è, —è–∫—â–æ –≤—ñ–Ω –≤—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π –Ω–∞ —á–∏—Å–ª–æ —ñ –∑–±—ñ–≥–∞—î—Ç—å—Å—è –∞–±–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–≤–∏—â—É—î –≤–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω–∏–π –ø–æ—Ä—ñ–≥.

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä    | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                   | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                        |
| ----------- | ---------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------- |
| `threshold` | `2`                          | –ì—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–Ω–µ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É.                               |
| `format`    | `'[$symbol$shlvl]($style) '` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                              |
| `symbol`    | `'‚ÜïÔ∏è  '`                     | –°–∏–º–≤–æ–ª, —è–∫–∏–π –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≤—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –¥–ª—è –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É `SHLVL`.           |
| `repeat`    | `false`                      | –ü–æ–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–Ω–æ –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É—î `symbol` –≤ –∫—ñ–ª—å–∫–æ—Å—Ç—ñ –∑–∞–∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω—ñ–π —É `SHLVL`. |
| `style`     | `'bold yellow'`              | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                               |
| `disabled`  | `true`                       | –í–∏–º–∏–∫–∞—î –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å `shlvl`.                                     |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥ | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| --------- | ------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| shlvl     | `3`     | –ü–æ—Ç–æ—á–Ω–µ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è `SHLVL`                 |
| symbol    |         | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\* |         | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[shlvl]
disabled = false
format = '$shlvl level(s) down'
threshold = 3
```

## Singularity

–ú–æ–¥—É–ª—å `singularity` –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É—î –ø–æ—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–π –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑ [Singularity](https://sylabs.io/singularity/), —è–∫—â–æ –≤–∏ –≤—Å–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∏–Ω—ñ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–π–Ω–µ—Ä–∞ —ñ `$SINGULARITY_NAME` –≤—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ.

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä   | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                       | –û–ø–∏—Å                                              |
| ---------- | -------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `format`   | `'[$symbol\[$env\]]($style) '` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                    |
| `symbol`   | `''`                             | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞, —â–æ –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥ –Ω–∞–∑–≤–æ—é –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑—É. |
| `style`    | `'bold dimmed blue'`             | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                     |
| `disabled` | `false`                          | –í–∏–º–∏–∫–∞—î –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å `singularity`.                     |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥      | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| --------- | ------------ | ---------------------------------------- |
| env       | `centos.img` | –ü–æ—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–π –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑ Singularity               |
| symbol    |              | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\* |              | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[singularity]
format = '[üì¶ \[$env\]]($style) '
```

## Solidity

The `solidity` module shows the currently installed version of [Solidity](https://soliditylang.org/) The module will be shown if any of the following conditions are met:

- The current directory contains a file with the `.sol` extension

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä            | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                           | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                              |
| ------------------- | ------------------------------------ | ----------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `format`            | `"via [$symbol($version )]($style)"` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                    |
| `version_format`    | `"v${major}.${minor}.${patch}"`      | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –≤–µ—Ä—Å—ñ—ó. –î–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω—ñ –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ `raw`, `major`, `minor` —Ç–∞ `patch` |
| `symbol`            | `"S "`                               | A format string representing the symbol of Solidity               |
| `compiler          | ["solc"]                             | The default compiler for Solidity.                                |
| `detect_extensions` | `["sol"]`                            | –Ø–∫—ñ —Ä–æ–∑—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ–≤–∏–Ω–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_files`      | `[]`                                 | –Ø–∫—ñ —ñ–º–µ–Ω–∞ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ–≤ –º–∞—é—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_folders`    | `[]`                                 | –í —è–∫–∏—Ö —Ç–µ–∫–∞—Ö —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å –º–∞—î –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏—Å—å.                          |
| `style`             | `"bold blue"`                        | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                     |
| `disabled`          | `false`                              | Disables this module.                                             |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥  | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| --------- | -------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| version   | `v0.8.1` | The version of `solidity`                |
| symbol    |          | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\* |          | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml
[solidity]
format = "via [S $version](blue bold)"
```

## Spack

The `spack` module shows the current [Spack](https://spack.readthedocs.io/en/latest/) environment, if `$SPACK_ENV` is set.

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä            | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                             | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                                                                                                                    |
| ------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `truncation_length` | `1`                                    | The number of directories the environment path should be truncated to. `0`¬†‚Äì –æ–∑–Ω–∞—á–∞—î –±–µ–∑ —Å–∫–æ—Ä–æ—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è. –¢–∞–∫–æ–∂ –ø–æ–¥–∏–≤—ñ—Ç—å—Å—è –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å [`directory`](#directory). |
| `symbol`            | `'üÖ¢  '`                                | –°–∏–º–≤–æ–ª —â–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥—É—î –Ω–∞–∑–≤—ñ –æ—Ç–æ—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è.                                                                                                                       |
| `style`             | `'bold blue'`                          | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                                                                                                           |
| `format`            | `'via [$symbol$environment]($style) '` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                                                                                                          |
| `disabled`          | `false`                                | Disables the `spack` module.                                                                                                                            |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞      | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥      | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| ----------- | ------------ | ---------------------------------------- |
| environment | `astronauts` | The current spack environment            |
| symbol      |              | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\*   |              | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[spack]
format = '[$symbol$environment](dimmed blue) '
```

## Status

The `status` module displays the exit code of the previous command. If $success_symbol is empty (default), the module will be shown only if the exit code is not `0`. The status code will cast to a signed 32-bit integer.

::: tip

–¶–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å —Ç–∏–ø–æ–≤–æ —î –≤–∏–º–∫–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–º. –©–æ–± –π–æ–≥–æ —É–≤—ñ–º–∫–Ω—É—Ç–∏, –≤—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤—ñ—Ç—å –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `disabled` –≤ `false` —É –≤–∞—à–æ–º—É —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ –Ω–∞–ª–∞—à—Ç—É–≤–∞–Ω—å.

:::

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä                    | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                                                                         | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                                  |
| --------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `format`                    | `'[$symbol$status]($style) '`                                                      | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è                                                         |
| `symbol`                    | `'‚ùå'`                                                                              | The symbol displayed on program error                                 |
| `success_symbol`            | `''`                                                                               | The symbol displayed on program success                               |
| `not_executable_symbol`     | `'üö´'`                                                                              | The symbol displayed when file isn't executable                       |
| `not_found_symbol`          | `'üîç'`                                                                              | The symbol displayed when the command can't be found                  |
| `sigint_symbol`             | `'üß±'`                                                                              | The symbol displayed on SIGINT (Ctrl + c)                             |
| `signal_symbol`             | `'‚ö°'`                                                                              | The symbol displayed on any signal                                    |
| `style`                     | `'bold red'`                                                                       | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                         |
| `recognize_signal_code`     | `true`                                                                             | Enable signal mapping from exit code                                  |
| `map_symbol`                | `false`                                                                            | Enable symbols mapping from exit code                                 |
| `pipestatus`                | `false`                                                                            | Enable pipestatus reporting                                           |
| `pipestatus_separator`      | <code>&vert;</code>                                                          | The symbol used to separate pipestatus segments (supports formatting) |
| `pipestatus_format`         | `'\[$pipestatus\] => [$symbol$common_meaning$signal_name$maybe_int]($style)'` | The format of the module when the command is a pipeline               |
| `pipestatus_segment_format` |                                                                                    | When specified, replaces `format` when formatting pipestatus segments |
| `disabled`                  | `true`                                                                             | Disables the `status` module.                                         |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞         | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥ | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                                                       |
| -------------- | ------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| status         | `127`   | The exit code of the last command                                                          |
| hex_status     | `0x7F`  | The exit code of the last command in hex                                                   |
| int            | `127`   | The exit code of the last command                                                          |
| common_meaning | `ERROR` | Meaning of the code if not a signal                                                        |
| signal_number  | `9`     | Signal number corresponding to the exit code, only if signalled                            |
| signal_name    | `KILL`  | Name of the signal corresponding to the exit code, only if signalled                       |
| maybe_int      | `7`     | Contains the exit code number when no meaning has been found                               |
| pipestatus     |         | Rendering of in pipeline programs' exit codes, this is only available in pipestatus_format |
| symbol         |         | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol`                                                   |
| style\*      |         | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`                                                    |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[status]
style = 'bg:blue'
symbol = 'üî¥ '
success_symbol = 'üü¢ SUCCESS'
format = '[\[$symbol$common_meaning$signal_name$maybe_int\]]($style) '
map_symbol = true
disabled = false
```

## Sudo

The `sudo` module displays if sudo credentials are currently cached. The module will only be shown if credentials are cached.

::: tip

–¶–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å —Ç–∏–ø–æ–≤–æ —î –≤–∏–º–∫–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–º. –©–æ–± –π–æ–≥–æ —É–≤—ñ–º–∫–Ω—É—Ç–∏, –≤—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤—ñ—Ç—å –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `disabled` –≤ `false` —É –≤–∞—à–æ–º—É —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ –Ω–∞–ª–∞—à—Ç—É–≤–∞–Ω—å.

:::

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä        | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ               | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                    |
| --------------- | ------------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------- |
| `format`        | `'[as $symbol]($style)'` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è                                           |
| `symbol`        | `'üßô '`                   | The symbol displayed when credentials are cached        |
| `style`         | `'bold blue'`            | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                           |
| `allow_windows` | `false`                  | Since windows has no default sudo, default is disabled. |
| `disabled`      | `true`                   | Disables the `sudo` module.                             |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥ | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| --------- | ------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| symbol    |         | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\* |         | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[sudo]
style = 'bold green'
symbol = 'üë©‚Äçüíª '
disabled = false
```

```toml
# On windows
# $HOME\.starship\config.toml

[sudo]
allow_windows = true
disabled = false
```

## Swift

By default the `swift` module shows the currently installed version of [Swift](https://swift.org/). –ú–æ–¥—É–ª—å –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è, —è–∫—â–æ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –±—É–¥—å-—è–∫–∞ –∑ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–∏—Ö —É–º–æ–≤:

- The current directory contains a `Package.swift` file
- The current directory contains a file with the `.swift` extension

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä            | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                           | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                              |
| ------------------- | ------------------------------------ | ----------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `format`            | `'via [$symbol($version )]($style)'` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                    |
| `version_format`    | `'v${raw}'`                          | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –≤–µ—Ä—Å—ñ—ó. –î–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω—ñ –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ `raw`, `major`, `minor` —Ç–∞ `patch` |
| `symbol`            | `'üê¶ '`                               | A format string representing the symbol of Swift                  |
| `detect_extensions` | `['swift']`                          | –Ø–∫—ñ —Ä–æ–∑—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ–≤–∏–Ω–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_files`      | `['Package.swift']`                  | –Ø–∫—ñ —ñ–º–µ–Ω–∞ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ–≤ –º–∞—é—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_folders`    | `[]`                                 | –í —è–∫–∏—Ö —Ç–µ–∫–∞—Ö —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å –º–∞—î –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏—Å—å.                          |
| `style`             | `'bold 202'`                         | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                     |
| `disabled`          | `false`                              | Disables the `swift` module.                                      |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥  | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| --------- | -------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| version   | `v5.2.4` | The version of `swift`                   |
| symbol    |          | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\* |          | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[swift]
format = 'via [üèé  $version](red bold)'
```

## Terraform

The `terraform` module shows the currently selected [Terraform workspace](https://www.terraform.io/docs/language/state/workspaces.html) and version.

::: tip

By default the Terraform version is not shown, since this is slow for current versions of Terraform when a lot of plugins are in use. If you still want to enable it, [follow the example shown below](#with-terraform-version).

:::

–¢–∏–ø–æ–≤–æ, –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è, —è–∫—â–æ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –±—É–¥—å-—è–∫–∞ –∑ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–∏—Ö —É–º–æ–≤:

- The current directory contains a `.terraform` folder
- Current directory contains a file with the `.tf`, `.tfplan` or `.tfstate` extensions

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä            | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                           | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                              |
| ------------------- | ------------------------------------ | ----------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `format`            | `'via [$symbol$workspace]($style) '` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞ –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                              |
| `version_format`    | `'v${raw}'`                          | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –≤–µ—Ä—Å—ñ—ó. –î–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω—ñ –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ `raw`, `major`, `minor` —Ç–∞ `patch` |
| `symbol`            | `'üí†'`                                | A format string shown before the terraform workspace.             |
| `detect_extensions` | `['tf', 'tfplan', 'tfstate']`        | –Ø–∫—ñ —Ä–æ–∑—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ–≤–∏–Ω–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_files`      | `[]`                                 | –Ø–∫—ñ —ñ–º–µ–Ω–∞ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ–≤ –º–∞—é—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_folders`    | `['.terraform']`                     | –í —è–∫–∏—Ö —Ç–µ–∫–∞—Ö —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å –º–∞—î –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏—Å—å.                          |
| `style`             | `'bold 105'`                         | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                     |
| `disabled`          | `false`                              | Disables the `terraform` module.                                  |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥    | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| --------- | ---------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| version   | `v0.12.24` | The version of `terraform`               |
| workspace | `default`  | The current Terraform workspace          |
| symbol    |            | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\* |            | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

#### With Terraform Version

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[terraform]
format = '[üèéüí® $version$workspace]($style) '
```

#### Without Terraform version

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[terraform]
format = '[üèéüí® $workspace]($style) '
```

## Time

The `time` module shows the current **local** time. The `format` configuration value is used by the [`chrono`](https://crates.io/crates/chrono) crate to control how the time is displayed. Take a look [at the chrono strftime docs](https://docs.rs/chrono/0.4.7/chrono/format/strftime/index.html) to see what options are available.

::: tip

–¶–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å —Ç–∏–ø–æ–≤–æ —î –≤–∏–º–∫–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–º. –©–æ–± –π–æ–≥–æ —É–≤—ñ–º–∫–Ω—É—Ç–∏, –≤—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤—ñ—Ç—å –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `disabled` –≤ `false` —É –≤–∞—à–æ–º—É —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ –Ω–∞–ª–∞—à—Ç—É–≤–∞–Ω—å.

:::

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä          | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ              | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                                                                                               |
| ----------------- | ----------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `format`          | `'at [$time]($style) '` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞ –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                                                                               |
| `use_12hr`        | `false`                 | Enables 12 hour formatting                                                                                                         |
| `time_format`     | see below               | The [chrono format string](https://docs.rs/chrono/0.4.7/chrono/format/strftime/index.html) used to format the time.                |
| `style`           | `'bold yellow'`         | The style for the module time                                                                                                      |
| `utc_time_offset` | `'local'`               | Sets the UTC offset to use. Range from -24 &lt; x &lt; 24. Allows floats to accommodate 30/45 minute timezone offsets. |
| `disabled`        | `true`                  | Disables the `time` module.                                                                                                        |
| `time_range`      | `'-'`                   | Sets the time range during which the module will be shown. Times must be specified in 24-hours format                              |

If `use_12hr` is `true`, then `time_format` defaults to `'%r'`. Otherwise, it defaults to `'%T'`. Manually setting `time_format` will override the `use_12hr` setting.

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥    | –û–ø–∏—Å                                    |
| --------- | ---------- | --------------------------------------- |
| time      | `13:08:10` | The current time.                       |
| style\* |            | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style` |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[time]
disabled = false
format = 'üïô[\[ $time \]]($style) '
time_format = '%T'
utc_time_offset = '-5'
time_range = '10:00:00-14:00:00'
```

## Username

The `username` module shows active user's username. –ú–æ–¥—É–ª—å –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è, —è–∫—â–æ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –±—É–¥—å-—è–∫–∞ –∑ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–∏—Ö —É–º–æ–≤:

- The current user is root/admin
- The current user isn't the same as the one that is logged in
- The user is currently connected as an SSH session
- The variable `show_always` is set to true

::: tip

SSH connection is detected by checking environment variables `SSH_CONNECTION`, `SSH_CLIENT`, and `SSH_TTY`. If your SSH host does not set up these variables, one workaround is to set one of them with a dummy value.

:::

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä      | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ              | –û–ø–∏—Å                                        |
| ------------- | ----------------------- | ------------------------------------------- |
| `style_root`  | `'bold red'`            | The style used when the user is root/admin. |
| `style_user`  | `'bold yellow'`         | The style used for non-root users.          |
| `format`      | `'[$user]($style) in '` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                              |
| `show_always` | `false`                 | Always shows the `username` module.         |
| `disabled`    | `false`                 | Disables the `username` module.             |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞  | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥      | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                                                        |
| ------- | ------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `style` | `'red bold'` | Mirrors the value of option `style_root` when root is logged in and `style_user` otherwise. |
| `user`  | `'matchai'`  | The currently logged-in user ID.                                                            |

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[username]
style_user = 'white bold'
style_root = 'black bold'
format = 'user: [$user]($style) '
disabled = false
show_always = true
```

## Vagrant

The `vagrant` module shows the currently installed version of [Vagrant](https://www.vagrantup.com/). –¢–∏–ø–æ–≤–æ, –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è, —è–∫—â–æ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –±—É–¥—å-—è–∫–∞ –∑ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–∏—Ö —É–º–æ–≤:

- The current directory contains a `Vagrantfile` file

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä            | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                           | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                              |
| ------------------- | ------------------------------------ | ----------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `format`            | `'via [$symbol($version )]($style)'` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                    |
| `version_format`    | `'v${raw}'`                          | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –≤–µ—Ä—Å—ñ—ó. –î–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω—ñ –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ `raw`, `major`, `minor` —Ç–∞ `patch` |
| `symbol`            | `'‚ç± '`                               | A format string representing the symbol of Vagrant.               |
| `detect_extensions` | `[]`                                 | –Ø–∫—ñ —Ä–æ–∑—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ–≤–∏–Ω–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_files`      | `['Vagrantfile']`                    | –Ø–∫—ñ —ñ–º–µ–Ω–∞ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ–≤ –º–∞—é—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_folders`    | `[]`                                 | –í —è–∫–∏—Ö —Ç–µ–∫–∞—Ö —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å –º–∞—î –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏—Å—å.                          |
| `style`             | `'cyan bold'`                        | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                     |
| `disabled`          | `false`                              | Disables the `vagrant` module.                                    |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥          | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| --------- | ---------------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| version   | `Vagrant 2.2.10` | The version of `Vagrant`                 |
| symbol    |                  | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\* |                  | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[vagrant]
format = 'via [‚ç± $version](bold white) '
```

## V

The `vlang` module shows you your currently installed version of [V](https://vlang.io/). –¢–∏–ø–æ–≤–æ, –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è, —è–∫—â–æ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –±—É–¥—å-—è–∫–∞ –∑ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–∏—Ö —É–º–æ–≤:

- The current directory contains a file with `.v` extension
- The current directory contains a `v.mod`, `vpkg.json` or `.vpkg-lock.json` file

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä            | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                                   | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                              |
| ------------------- | -------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `format`            | `'via [$symbol($version )]($style)'`         | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                    |
| `version_format`    | `'v${raw}'`                                  | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –≤–µ—Ä—Å—ñ—ó. –î–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω—ñ –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ `raw`, `major`, `minor` —Ç–∞ `patch` |
| `symbol`            | `'V '`                                       | A format string representing the symbol of V                      |
| `detect_extensions` | `['v']`                                      | –Ø–∫—ñ —Ä–æ–∑—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ–≤–∏–Ω–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_files`      | `['v.mod', 'vpkg.json', '.vpkg-lock.json' ]` | –Ø–∫—ñ —ñ–º–µ–Ω–∞ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ–≤ –º–∞—é—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_folders`    | `[]`                                         | –í —è–∫–∏—Ö —Ç–µ–∫–∞—Ö —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å –º–∞—î –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏—Å—å.                          |
| `style`             | `'blue bold'`                                | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                     |
| `disabled`          | `false`                                      | Disables the `vlang` module.                                      |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥ | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| --------- | ------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| version   | `v0.2`  | The version of `v`                       |
| symbol    |         | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\* |         | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml
[vlang]
format = 'via [V $version](blue bold) '
```

## VCSH

The `vcsh` module displays the current active [VCSH](https://github.com/RichiH/vcsh) repository. The module will be shown only if a repository is currently in use.

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä   | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                       | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                   |
| ---------- | -------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------ |
| `symbol`   | `''`                             | The symbol used before displaying the repository name. |
| `style`    | `'bold yellow'`                  | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                          |
| `format`   | `'vcsh [$symbol$repo]($style) '` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                         |
| `disabled` | `false`                          | Disables the `vcsh` module.                            |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥                                     | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| --------- | ------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| repo      | `dotfiles` if in a VCSH repo named dotfiles | The active repository name               |
| symbol    |                                             | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\* | `black bold dimmed`                         | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[vcsh]
format = '[üÜÖ $repo](bold blue) '
```

## Zig

By default the `zig` module shows the currently installed version of [Zig](https://ziglang.org/). –ú–æ–¥—É–ª—å –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è, —è–∫—â–æ –≤–∏–∫–æ–Ω—É—î—Ç—å—Å—è –±—É–¥—å-—è–∫–∞ –∑ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–∏—Ö —É–º–æ–≤:

- The current directory contains a `.zig` file

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä            | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                           | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                              |
| ------------------- | ------------------------------------ | ----------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `format`            | `'via [$symbol($version )]($style)'` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                    |
| `version_format`    | `'v${raw}'`                          | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –≤–µ—Ä—Å—ñ—ó. –î–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω—ñ –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ `raw`, `major`, `minor` —Ç–∞ `patch` |
| `symbol`            | `'‚ÜØ '`                               | The symbol used before displaying the version of Zig.             |
| `style`             | `'bold yellow'`                      | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                     |
| `disabled`          | `false`                              | Disables the `zig` module.                                        |
| `detect_extensions` | `['zig']`                            | –Ø–∫—ñ —Ä–æ–∑—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–æ–≤–∏–Ω–Ω—ñ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_files`      | `[]`                                 | –Ø–∫—ñ —ñ–º–µ–Ω–∞ —Ñ–∞–π–ª—ñ–≤ –º–∞—é—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏ —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å.                      |
| `detect_folders`    | `[]`                                 | –í —è–∫–∏—Ö —Ç–µ–∫–∞—Ö —Ü–µ–π –º–æ–¥—É–ª—å –º–∞—î –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç–∏—Å—å.                          |

### –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω—ñ

| –ó–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞    | –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥  | –û–ø–∏—Å                                     |
| --------- | -------- | ---------------------------------------- |
| version   | `v0.6.0` | The version of `zig`                     |
| symbol    |          | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `symbol` |
| style\* |          | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[zig]
symbol = '‚ö°Ô∏è '
```

## Custom commands

The `custom` modules show the output of some arbitrary commands.

These modules will be shown if any of the following conditions are met:

- The current directory contains a file whose name is in `detect_files`
- The current directory contains a directory whose name is in `detect_folders`
- The current directory contains a file whose extension is in `detect_extensions`
- The `when` command returns 0
- The current Operating System (std::env::consts::OS) matches with `os` field if defined.

::: tip

Multiple custom modules can be defined by using a `.`.

:::

::: tip

The order in which custom modules are shown can be individually set by including `${custom.foo}` in the top level `format` (as it includes a dot, you need to use `${...}`). By default, the `custom` module will simply show all custom modules in the order they were defined.

:::

::: tip

[Issue #1252](https://github.com/starship/starship/discussions/1252) contains examples of custom modules. If you have an interesting example not covered there, feel free to share it there!

:::

::: warning Command output is printed unescaped to the prompt

Whatever output the command generates is printed unmodified in the prompt. This means if the output contains special sequences that are interpreted by your shell they will be expanded when displayed. These special sequences are shell specific, e.g. you can write a command module that writes bash sequences, e.g. `\h`, but this module will not work in a fish or zsh shell.

Format strings can also contain shell specific prompt sequences, e.g. [Bash](https://www.gnu.org/software/bash/manual/html_node/Controlling-the-Prompt.html), [Zsh](https://zsh.sourceforge.io/Doc/Release/Prompt-Expansion.html).

:::

### –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏

| –ü–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä            | –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ                      | –û–ø–∏—Å                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| ------------------- | ------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `command`           | `''`                            | The command whose output should be printed. The command will be passed on stdin to the shell.                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| `when`              | `false`                         | Either a boolean value (`true` or `false`, without quotes) or a string shell command used as a condition to show the module. In case of a string, the module will be shown if the command returns a `0` status code.                                                                          |
| `require_repo`      | `false`                         | If `true`, the module will only be shown in paths containing a (git) repository. This option alone is not sufficient display condition in absence of other options.                                                                                                                           |
| `shell`             |                                 | [See below](#custom-command-shell)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `description`       | `'<custom module>'`       | The description of the module that is shown when running `starship explain`.                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `detect_files`      | `[]`                            | The files that will be searched in the working directory for a match.                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `detect_folders`    | `[]`                            | The directories that will be searched in the working directory for a match.                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `detect_extensions` | `[]`                            | The extensions that will be searched in the working directory for a match.                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `symbol`            | `''`                            | The symbol used before displaying the command output.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `style`             | `'bold green'`                  | –°—Ç–∏–ª—å –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| `format`            | `'[$symbol($output )]($style)'` | –§–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ç –º–æ–¥—É–ª—è.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `disabled`          | `false`                         | Disables this `custom` module.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `os`                |                                 | Operating System name on which the module will be shown (unix, linux, macos, windows, ... ) [See possible values](https://doc.rust-lang.org/std/env/consts/constant.OS.html).                                                                                                                 |
| `use_stdin`         |                                 | An optional boolean value that overrides whether commands should be forwarded to the shell via the standard input or as an argument. If unset standard input is used by default, unless the shell does not support it (cmd, nushell). Setting this disables shell-specific argument handling. |
| `ignore_timeout`    | `false`                         | Ignore global `command_timeout` setting and keep running external commands, no matter how long they take.                                                                                                                                                                                     |

| style\* | –í—ñ–¥–¥–∑–µ—Ä–∫–∞–ª—é—î –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–Ω—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞ `style`  |

*: –¶—è –∑–º—ñ–Ω–Ω–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ –±—É—Ç–∏ –≤–∏–∫–æ—Ä–∏—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞ –ª–∏—à–µ —è–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–Ω–∞ —Å—Ç–∏–ª—é —Ä—è–¥–∫–∞

#### Custom command shell

`shell` accepts a non-empty list of strings, where:

- The first string is the path to the shell to use to execute the command.
- Other following arguments are passed to the shell.

If unset, it will fallback to STARSHIP_SHELL and then to 'sh' on Linux, and 'cmd /C' on Windows.

The `command` will be passed in on stdin.

If `shell` is not given or only contains one element and Starship detects PowerShell will be used, the following arguments will automatically be added: `-NoProfile -Command -`. If `shell` is not given or only contains one element and Starship detects Cmd will be used, the following argument will automatically be added: `/C` and `stdin` will be set to `false`. If `shell` is not given or only contains one element and Starship detects Nushell will be used, the following arguments will automatically be added: `-c` and `stdin` will be set to `false`. This behavior can be avoided by explicitly passing arguments to the shell, e.g.

```toml
shell = ['pwsh', '-Command', '-']
```

::: warning Make sure your custom shell configuration exits gracefully

If you set a custom command, make sure that the default Shell used by starship will properly execute the command with a graceful exit (via the `shell` option).

For example, PowerShell requires the `-Command` parameter to execute a one liner. Omitting this parameter might throw starship into a recursive loop where the shell might try to load a full profile environment with starship itself again and hence re-execute the custom command, getting into a never ending loop.

Parameters similar to `-NoProfile` in PowerShell are recommended for other shells as well to avoid extra loading time of a custom profile on every starship invocation.

Automatic detection of shells and proper parameters addition are currently implemented, but it's possible that not all shells are covered. [Please open an issue](https://github.com/starship/starship/issues/new/choose) with shell details and starship configuration if you hit such scenario.

:::

### –ü—Ä–∏–∫–ª–∞–¥

```toml
# ~/.config/starship.toml

[custom.foo]
command = 'echo foo' # shows output of command
detect_files = ['foo'] # can specify filters but wildcards are not supported
when = ''' test "$HOME" = "$PWD" '''
format = ' transcending [$output]($style)'

[custom.time]
command = 'time /T'
detect_extensions = ['pst'] # filters *.pst files
shell = ['pwsh.exe', '-NoProfile', '-Command', '-']

[custom.time-as-arg]
command = 'time /T'
detect_extensions = ['pst'] # filters *.pst files
shell = ['pwsh.exe', '-NoProfile', '-Command']
use_stdin = false
```
